commit fcab7adc64a54dad94ae63b67c60ad2bc2cb7c20
Author: Thiemo Müller <thiemo@edge-box.com>
Date:   Thu Sep 10 16:09:39 2020 +0200

    fix(syndication): improve reliability of new hashing by using it in the push controller as well
    
    Before, the syndication would still use the changed timestamp of the entities. Now it uses the new entity hash available per entity, saves it to the entity status and also logs it to Drupals watchdog.

commit b6f6c24ef988159ac2c1c0411428cab1264e57e5
Author: Thiemo Müller <thiemo@edge-box.com>
Date:   Thu Sep 10 14:36:22 2020 +0200

    feat(syndication): add a unique version hash of an entity wherever it is referenced
    
    This ensures that the entity content actually changes and triggers another syndication to remote sites at the Sync Core. The aim is to improve reliability of nested entities where parent entities aren't updated directly.

commit 0f1132d56847e40c1eeb00670b7912dcea7f6337

commit d65abd73f421b24d6fd2772dbb97f5bb936b62e0
Author: Thiemo Müller <thiemo@edge-box.com>
Date:   Wed Aug 26 09:05:05 2020 +0200

    fix(flow-export): export condition for all flows for the same entity type
    
    Previously when exporting Flows that overlapped for pulling the same entity type, the condition would only be applied to the first Flow. All following Flows would not have their condition ('subscribe only to' filter) applied.

commit ef6428508a7798f294f8f783bbbb76eda77e526f
Author: Thiemo Müller <thiemo@edge-box.com>
Date:   Fri Aug 14 10:27:30 2020 +0200

    fix(export): ensure entity types are only defined once per site
    
    When configuring multiple Flows that use the same entity types and the same Pool, the Entity Type may still only be defined once. Otherwise syndications of the duplicated entity type would randomly succeed or fail.

commit a94645c6f42f2a112f3ed2832400401b5cfbf49b
Author: Thiemo Müller <thiemo@edge-box.com>
Date:   Thu Aug 13 11:10:23 2020 +0200

    fix(export): use identical logic for older and newer drush
    
    Added a count to tell the user how many Flows were exported to give adequate feedback. Not using the same logic in drush may have caused an issue with exporting flows that are only enabled through the settings.php file.

commit 77f71037c1ccc0ffdc7e75b1c032ff89d958d0a6
Author: Thiemo Müller <thiemo@edge-box.com>
Date:   Thu Aug 13 10:42:00 2020 +0200

    feat(pool): allow changing pool assignment for a whole flow
    
    When you're adding a new pool to the site we can only guess what assignment you want for the pool in existing flow configurations. With the new form you can add a pool and then assign the correct behavior to it per flow. It also allows you to change the behavior of existing pools in case you made a configuration mistake and don't want to go through every entity type individually.

commit dd684ece5d7360df0e71883aecdd6ca938ffa07e
Author: Thiemo Müller <thiemo@edge-box.com>
Date:   Thu Aug 13 10:14:10 2020 +0200

    refactor(flow): add type with constants to flow entity class
    
    Use constants to avoid errors from using simple strings. Use a method at the Flow entity to re-use it at other places.

commit f1ff387ac3400f32b76580c80ca8edfc85205213
Author: Thiemo Müller <thiemo@edge-box.com>
Date:   Thu Aug 13 09:08:37 2020 +0200

    fix(networking): move check whether the Sync Core can access a site to Flow form validation rather than Pool form validation
    
    If a site only pushes content but doesn't pull content, the Sync Core doesn't require access to the site. So with the new validation private staging instances won't complain about missing site access from the Sync Core. To allow local configuration of Flows without Sync Core access, users can also set the Flow to be inactive in which case saving the Flow despite the Sync Core not having access to the site is possible.
